#!/usr/bin/python2.7
# Attempting to allow use of Python3.X hard Python
# filename is rpasm27.txt and is in Python 2.7 or 3.4
# 2120 rj1760 is still broken
# stuck at line 3957 > 255
# stuck at line 1261  or rrd1370 is BROKEN
# attempting to translate casm5.c into pasm27.py
def mids(strids,plonepos,midsw):
 plzerpos=plonepos-1
 rids=""
 idsctr=0
 while idsctr < midsw:
  ridt=""
  rid633=idsctr+plzerpos
  if rid633 >= 0 and rid633 < len(strids):
   ridt=strids[idsctr+plzerpos]
  rids=rids+(""+ridt)
  idsctr=idsctr+1
 rrids=""+rids
 return rrids
def areadline(hantalia4):
 arrel=ispy23()
 arlcy=""
 arlctr=0
 arla=1
 while arla == 1:
  arltny=""
  arldl=""
  if arrel == 2:
   try:
    arldl=hantalia4.read(1)
   except:
    arltny=""
  if arrel == 3:
   try:
    arldx=hantalia4.read(1)
    arldw=str(arldx)
    arldl=""
    if len(arldw) >= 4:
     arldl=mids(arldw,3,1)
     if arldl == canstri(92) and mids(arldw,4,1) == canstri(110):
      arla=0
     if arldl == canstri(92):
      arldl=""
   except EOFError:
    arltny=""
    arla=0
   except:
    arltny=""
    arla=0
  if arrel == 2 and len(arldl) > 0:
   arltny=mids(arldl,1,1)
  if arrel == 3 and len(arldl) > 0 and arla == 1:
   arltny=mids(arldl,1,1)
  if len(arltny) == 1 and canintsone(arltny) >= 14:
   arlcy=arlcy+canstri(canintsone(arltny))
  arlctr=arlctr+1
  if arltny == chr(10) or arlctr >= 80:
   arla=0
# if arlcy == ";@FIN":
#  arlcy=""
# delimiter is no longer needed because end of file is detected by
# 3 bytes being returned from read instead of 4 for the one byte
# at last-1 in Python 3.X
 return arlcy
def initlkey(keroeone):
 hasone=0
 if hasattr(__builtins__,"raw_input"):
  interin=raw_input
  ATRSUFFIX="Python_2.7_?"
  hasone=1
 if hasone == 0:
  interin=input
  ATRSUFFIX="Python_3.4_?"
 if keroeone == 1:
  interin=ATRSUFFIX
 return interin
def ispy23():
 irpy34=3
 if hasattr(__builtins__,"raw_input"):
  irpy34=2
 return irpy34
def line_input(atrpom):
 nameofin=initlkey(0)
 ttrpom=atrpom+initlkey(1)
 nfin=nameofin(ttrpom)
 return nfin
def scrprint(scpstr,scpzub,scplen):
 scpctr=0
 scptran=chr(32)
 scpwtr=""
 scpa=1
 scpl=len(scpstr)
 scpzen=scplen
 if scplen > scpl:
  scpzen=scpl
 while scpa == 1:
  scpraw=scpctr+scpzub
  scplast=scptran
  if scpraw < 0 or scpraw >= scpl:
   scpa=0
  if scpraw >= 0 and scpraw < scpl:
   scpsub=sc(scpraw,scpl,58)
   scprran=scpstr[scpsub]
   scptran=scprran
   try:
    scptran=chr(scprran)
   except:
    scptran=scprran
   scptram=scptran
   if scptran == chr(33):
    scpa=0
   if scptran < chr(32):
    scptram=chr(59)
   if scptran >= chr(1) and scptran <= chr(9):
    scptram=chr(48+ord(scptran))
#   scpa=0
   if scptran == chr(46) and scplast == chr(46):
    scpa=0
  if scpa == 1:
   scpwtr=scpwtr+str(scptram)
   scpctr=scpctr+1
   if scpctr >= scpzen:
    scpa=0
 print(scpwtr)
 return 0
# for u
def uxfill():
 ux=" 0 1 2 3 DQ RESQ DD RESD "
 ux=ux+" DB DW RESB RESW ORG STAC"
 ux=ux+"KEND STACKORG NEGORG "
# // 2300 REM compiler directives two jumps
 ux=ux+" ADD OR ADC SBB AND SUB XOR CMP "
# // 2304 REM 2302 imed 100000dw mduuuram%+8*irem8%
# // non imed uses 0+8*erem8%
# // 2306 REM 2308 MOV imed c6+emw% md000r/m,
# // 88+2*emd%+emw% seg, 8c+emd*2
 ux=ux+" MOV y y y y y y 31 "
 ux=ux+" PUSH y y y y y y 39 "
# // 2312 REM PUSH 1010reg lastpos=32, word
# // ff md 110 r/m  segment*8+6
 ux=ux+" POP y y y y y y 47 "
# // 2316 REM pop 1011reg lastpos%=32,word
# // 8f md000r/m,7+seg*8 (NOT CS)
 ux=ux+" INC DEC y y y y y y y y y y y y y 63 "
# //  2320 REM 2318 irem8%*8+40h+reg
# // lastpos%=32,byte fe+emw% md(emw%*8)R/M
# // 2322 REM 2324 GOTO ON CONDITION
# // USES irem16% instead of irem8%
 ux=ux+" JV JNV JB  JNB JE  JNE JBE JNBE "
 ux=ux+"  JS  JNS JPE JPO JL  JNL JNG  JNLE "
 ux=ux+" JO JNO JNAE JAE JZ JNZ JNA JA   "
 ux=ux+"  JN  JNN JP  JNP JNGE JGE JLE JG   "
# // 2332 REM SEG OVERRIDE =26+8*segreg
 ux=ux+" ES CS SS DS y y y 103 "
 ux=ux+" RET  RETF y y y y y 111 "
# // 2338 REM 2336 c2+8*irem8%,
# // (add 1 if lasttype%<>1 not imed
 ux=ux+" ROL ROR RCL RCR SHL SHR 118 SAR "
 ux=ux+" ROL ROR RCL RCR SAL SHR 126 SAR "
# // 2344 REM 2340 shifts d0+v*2+emw%
# // MD(8*irem8%)R/M lasttype%=1 for v=0
 ux=ux+" LEA y y y y y y 135 "
# // 2348 REM LEA 8D MDREGR/M
# // 2350 REM 2352 single byte
# // instructions 9c+irem8%*1
 ux=ux+" PUSHF POPF SAHF LAHF y y y 143 "
# // REM call 2358 imed linepat&=4G211
# // call far 9a(5) linepat&=4G22 rel e8(3)
# // 56 REM mduuuram%<256 (xrbase-16)="F"
# // far or near indirect  jmp same rules
 ux=ux+" CALL y y y y y y 151 "
 ux=ux+" JMP   y y y y y y 159 "
# // 2362 REM 2364 TEST IMED f6+emw%
# // md000r/m, 84+emw% MDREGR/M
 ux=ux+" TEST y y y y y y 167 "
# // 2366 REM 2368 IN E4 + erem8%*1 + emw%,
# // add 8 IF not imed
 ux=ux+" IN y OUT y y y y 175 "
# //  2370 REM  2372 CE + irem8%*1
 ux=ux+" INTO IRET y y y y y 183 "
# // 2374 REM 2376 CD+immediate
# //  needs immediate number byte
 ux=ux+" INT y y y y y y 191 "
# // 2378 REM 2380 single byte
# // character series a4+irem16%
 ux=ux+" MOVSB MOVSW CMPSB CMPSW y 1"
 ux=ux+"97 STOSB STOSW "
 ux=ux+" LODSB LODSW SCASB SC"
 ux=ux+"ASW y y y 207       "
# // 2384 REM 2386 F6 + emw%,C0+irem8%*8
# // regsingle or irem8%*8+mduuuram%
 ux=ux+" y y NOT NEG y y y 215 "
# // 2388 REM 2390 NOP 90
 ux=ux+" NOP y y y y y y 223 "
# // 2392 REM 2394 loopne series
# // realative jump E0+erem8%*1
 ux=ux+" LOOPNE LOOPE LOOP JCXZ y y y 231 "
# // 2396 REM 2398 LES C4+irem8%*1,
# // mduuuram%+xxregxxx%
 ux=ux+" LES LDS y y y y y 239 "
# // 2400 REM 2402 lock series
# // F0+irem8%*1 single byte
 ux=ux+" LOCK y REPNZ REPZ HALT CMC y 247 "
# // 2404 REM 2406 duplicate lock series for REP
 ux=ux+" LOCK y REPNZ REP  HALT CMC y 255 "
# // 2408 REM 2410 CLC SERIES
# // F8+irem8%*1 single byte instructions
 ux=ux+" CLC STC CLI STI CLD STD y 263 "
# // 2412 REM 2414 F6+emw%,mduuuram%+irem8%*8
 ux=ux+" 264 y y 267 MUL IMUL DIV IDIV "
# // 2416 REM 2418 XCHG 86+emw%,mduuuram%+xxregxxx%
 ux=ux+" xchg y y y y y y 279 "
# // 2420 REM 2422 27+irem8%*8 unknown byte group
 ux=ux+" DAA DAS AAA AAS y y y 287 "
# // 2426 REM 2428 D4+irem8%*1
# // unknown immediate8 group
 ux=ux+" AAM AAD y y y y y 295 "
# // 2430 REM 2432 xlatb d7
 ux=ux+" XLATB y y y y y y 303 "
# // 2434 REM 2436 cbw single byte
# // series 98+irem8%*1
 ux=ux+" CBW CWD y WAIT y y y 311 "
 ux=ux+" BITS ALIGN SYMDIFF REALSE"
 ux=ux+"GDIFF SECTION y y 319 "
 ux=ux+" ..... ";
# // 2438 REM end of known integer
# // instruction list for 8088
 return ux
# for listreg[]
def ulrfill():
 ulr="R0R1R2R3R4R5R6R7"
 ulr=ulr+"AXCXDXBXSPBPSIDI"
 ulr=ulr+"ALCLDLBLAHCHDHBHESCSSSDSRCRDRERF......."
 return ulr

# def sc(long tyresub,long tyremax,long tyreln):
def sc(tyresub,tyremax,tyreln):
 tyrewub=tyremax-1
# wrong tyresub=tyremax-1
# tyrewub=tyremax-1;
#  if(tyresub < 0)goto tyrefail39;
#  if(tyresub >= tyremax)goto tyrefail39;
 if tyresub < 0 or tyresub >= tyremax:
  print("tyresub = "+str(tyresub)+"    tyremax = "+str(tyremax))
  print("***ERROR*** in sc at line "+str(tyreln))
  exit()
 if tyresub >= 0 and tyresub < tyremax:
  tyrewub=tyresub
 if tyresub < 0:
  tyrewub=0
 return tyrewub
#  tyrewub=tyresub;
#  goto tyrebot41;
# tyrefail39:  aerrorln=tyreln;
# // insert debugger trigger
# // crash in 32 bit mode here
# tyrebot41:  if(tyresub<0)tyrewub=0;
#  return tyrewub;
#  }
# bootom of sc 432

#  long iamfromc(char wasac)

#  long iumfromc;
def iamfromc(wasac):
 iumfromc=wasac
 if iumfromc < 0:
  iumfromc=iumfromc+256
 return iumfromc
#  iumfromc=(long)wasac;

# bottom of iamfromc 449
#  char canminus(long wasai)
#  {
#  char cbnminus;
#  if(wasai < 128)cbnminus=(char)wasai;
#  if(wasai > 127)cbnminus=(char)(wasai-256);
#  return cbnminus;
#  }
def canminus(wasai):
 cbnminus=chr(0)
 if wasai < 128 and wasai >= 0:
  cbnminus=chr(wasai)
 if wasai > 127:
  cbnminus=chr(wasai)
 if wasai < 0:
  cbnminus=chr(wasai+256)
# not in Python  cbnminus=chr(wasai-256)
 return cbnminus
# end of canminus 464
def canbyte(wazai):
 cbtempa=bytearray(1 * [0])
 wazaip=0
 if wazai < 0:
  wazaip=wazai+256
 if wazai >= 0:
  wazaip=wazai
 cbtempa[0]=wazaip
 wazair=cbtempa[0]
 return wazair
def canintsone(stroneca):
 cisonerz=0
 if len(stroneca) == 1:
  cisonerz=ord(stroneca)
  if cisonerz < 0:
   cisonerz=cisonerz+256
 return cisonerz
def canstri(watai):
 rzcans=""
 rzcann=""
 cbtempb=bytearray(1 * [0])
 cbtempb[0]=canbyte(watai)
 rzcant=str(cbtempb)
 if len(rzcant) == 1:
  rzcann=rzcant
 if len(rzcant) == 15 or len(rzcant) == 16:
  rzcann=rzcant[12]
 rzcans=""+rzcann
 return rzcans
def canbys(wsts):
 cbytmp=canintsone(wsts)
 cbyres=canbyte(cbytmp)
 return cbyres
